        let noResultsGa = srpDataLayerManager.addNoSearchResultsEvent;
        let optMnger = window["optimizelyManager"];
        if(optMnger !== null  && optMnger !== void 0 && optMnger.isFeatureEnabled('enable_srp_listings_redesign_dt')) {
            noResultsGa = srpDataLayerManager.addNoSearchResultsEventRedesign;
        }

        if (domLoad) {
                    }
    }
    Trader.initLazyLoad = function() {
        var lazyLoad = new LazyLoad(), body;
        lazyLoad.update();
        body = $("html, body");
        window.scroll(0, body.scrollTop() + 2);
    }
</script>
